<script>
(function() {
    /*base*/
    var Base = {
        $ : function(id){
            return document.getElementById(id);
        },
        addEventListener : function(element, type, handler) {
            if (element.addEventListener) {
                element.addEventListener(type, handler, false);
            } else if (element.attachEvent) {
                element.attachEvent('on' + type, handler);
            } else {
                element['on' + type] = handler;
            }
        },
        createElement : function(tagName, attributes) {
            var element = document.createElement(tagName);
            for (var attributeName in attributes) {
                element[attributeName] = attributes[attributeName];
            }
            return element;
        },
        trim : function(s) {
            if(s.trim) {
                return s.trim();
            }
            return s.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/, '');
        }
    };

    var kwInput = Base.$('keyword');

    // è®¾ç½®è¾å¥æ¡ç¦ç¹
    kwInput.focus();

	function getSid() {
		var match = document.cookie.match(/QiHooGUID=([^;]*)/);
		if (match) {
			return match[1];
		}
		return '';
	}
    function html_encode(str){     
        if (str.length == 0) return "";   
        var result = str.replace(/&/g, "&amp;")
                .replace(/</g, "&lt;")
                .replace(/>/g, "&gt;")
                .replace(/ /g, "&nbsp;")
                .replace(/\'/g, "&#39;")
                .replace(/\"/g, "&quot;");   
        return result;   
    } 

	/*
	404é¡µé¢æç´¢æ¡suggstç¹å»ç»è®¡ URL015
	*/
	Base.addEventListener(document.getElementById('suggest-align'), 'mousedown', function(event) {
		event = event || window.event;
		var target = event.srcElement || event.target,
			item = null;

		if (target.tagName.toUpperCase() === 'LI') {
			item = target;
		}
		if (target.parentNode.tagName.toUpperCase() === 'LI') {
			item = target.parentNode;
		}
		// cb.onselectitem
		if (monitor && item) {
			monitor.setConf('clickUrl', '//s.360.cn/sou/suggest.gif').log({
				pro: 'so_com',
				pid: '404',
				mod: 'suggest',
				input: kwInput.value,
				click: item.getAttribute('acvalue'),
				pos: item.getAttribute('ac_index'),
				sguid: getSid()
			}, 'click');
		}
	});

	/*æ¾ç¤º404url*/
    var decodeUrl;
    try{
        decodeUrl = decodeURIComponent(location.href);
    } catch(e){
        decodeUrl = location.href;
    }
	Base.$('url_404').innerHTML = html_encode(decodeUrl);

    //ç»å®åæ¢æç´¢å¼ææé®hoverçå¬
    var moreDiv = Base.$('g-hd-searchs'),
            moreUl = Base.$('mod-engs');
    if(moreDiv) {
        var timer;
        var enter = function() {
            clearTimeout(timer);
            timer = setTimeout(function(){
                moreUl.style.display = "block";
            }, 300);
        };
        var leave = function() {
            clearTimeout(timer);
            timer = setTimeout(function() {
                moreUl.style.display = "none";
            } , 300);
        };
        Base.addEventListener(moreDiv , "mouseenter" , enter);
        Base.addEventListener(moreDiv , "mouseleave" , leave);
    }
})();
</script>

<script>
createSuggest({
